    @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] != null)
    {
        <div class="alert alert-success alert-dismissible fade show" role="alert">
            @TempData["SuccessMessage"]
            <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="alert" aria-label="Close"></button>
        </div>
    }

    <div class="accordion" id="pointsAccordion">
        @foreach (var dept in Model.DepartmentReports)
        {
            var collapseId = $"collapse{dept.DeptName.Replace(" ", "")}";
            var headingId = $"heading{dept.DeptName.Replace(" ", "")}";

            <div class="accordion-item">
                <h2 class="accordion-header" id="@headingId">
                    <button class="accordion-button collapsed" type="button" data-bs-toggle="collapse" data-bs-target="#@collapseId" aria-expanded="false" aria-controls="@collapseId">
                        <span class="fw-bold me-auto">@dept.DeptName</span>
                        <span class="badge bg-primary rounded-pill">Total Points: @dept.TotalPoints</span>
                    </button>
                </h2>
                <div id="@collapseId" class="accordion-collapse collapse" aria-labelledby="@headingId">
                    <div class="accordion-body">
                        @if (dept.MatchDetails.Any())
                        {
                            <div class="table-responsive">
                                <table class="table table-sm table-bordered">
                                    <thead class="table-light">
                                        <tr>
                                            <th>Date</th>
                                            <th>Sport</th>
                                            <th>Opponent</th>
                                            <th>Score</th>
                                            <th>Result</th>
                                            <th>Points</th>
                                        </tr>
                                    </thead>
                                    <tbody>
                                        @foreach (var match in dept.MatchDetails)
                                        {
                                            <tr class="@(match.Outcome == "Win" ? "table-success" : (match.Outcome == "Draw" ? "table-warning" : "table-light"))">
                                                <td>@match.MatchDate.ToShortDateString()</td>
                                                <td>@match.SportName</td>
                                                <td>@match.OpponentName</td>
                                                <td>@match.ScoreResult</td>
                                                <td>@match.Outcome</td>
                                                <td><strong>@match.PointsAwarded</strong></td>
                                            </tr>
                                        }
                                    </tbody>
                                </table>
                            </div>
                        }
                        else
                        {
                            <p class="text-muted fst-italic">No finished matches found for this department.</p>
                        }
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        }
    </div>

    <div class="mt-4 text-center">
        <a asp-action="Dashboard" class="btn btn-secondary">Back to Dashboard</a>
    </div>
</div>

./Views/Admin/UpdateCaptains.cshtml
@model SportsPortal.Models.UpdateCaptainViewModel

@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Update Captains";
    Layout = "_LayoutAdmin";
}

<div class="container py-4">
    <h1 class="text-center mb-5 display-4 text-primary">Update Captains</h1>

    @if (TempData["SuccessMessage"] != null)
    {
        <div class="alert alert-success alert-dismissible fade show" role="alert">
            @TempData["SuccessMessage"]
            <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="alert" aria-label="Close"></button>
        </div>
    }
    @if (TempData["ErrorMessage"] != null)
    {
        <div class="alert alert-danger alert-dismissible fade show" role="alert">
            @TempData["ErrorMessage"]
            <button type="button" class="btn-close" data-bs-dismiss="alert" aria-label="Close"></button>
        </div>
    }

    <div class="row justify-content-center">
        <div class="col-md-8 col-lg-6">
            <div class="card shadow-lg p-4">
                <form asp-action="UpdateCaptains" method="post">
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label asp-for="SelectedDepartmentId" class="form-label">Department</label>
                        <select asp-for="SelectedDepartmentId" asp-items="@Model.Departments" class="form-select">
                            <option value="">-- Select Department --</option>
                        </select>
                        <span asp-validation-for="SelectedDepartmentId" class="text-danger"></span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label asp-for="SelectedSportId" class="form-label">Sport</label>
                        <select asp-for="SelectedSportId" asp-items="@Model.Sports" class="form-select">
                            <option value="">-- Select Sport --</option>
                        </select>
                        <span asp-validation-for="SelectedSportId" class="text-danger"></span>
                    </div>

                    <div id="captainInfo" class="mb-3" style="display: none;">
                        <p>Current Captain: <strong id="currentCaptainName"></strong> (Player ID: <span id="currentCaptainId"></span>)</p>
                    </div>

                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label asp-for="NewCaptainFullName" class="form-label">New Captain Full Name</label>
                        <input asp-for="NewCaptainFullName" class="form-control" />
                        <span asp-validation-for="NewCaptainFullName" class="text-danger"></span>
                    </div>
                    <div class="mb-3">
                        <label asp-for="NewCaptainRegNumber" class="form-label">New Captain Registration Number (Optional)</label>
                        <input asp-for="NewCaptainRegNumber" class="form-control" type="number" />
                        <span asp-validation-for="NewCaptainRegNumber" class="text-danger"></span>
                    </div>

                    <div class="d-grid gap-2">
                        <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg">Update Captain</button>
                    </div>
                </form>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    @{await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");}
    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            const departmentSelect = document.getElementById('SelectedDepartmentId');
            const sportSelect = document.getElementById('SelectedSportId');
            const captainInfoDiv = document.getElementById('captainInfo');
            const currentCaptainNameSpan = document.getElementById('currentCaptainName');
            const currentCaptainIdSpan = document.getElementById('currentCaptainId');
            const newCaptainFullNameInput = document.getElementById('NewCaptainFullName');

            async function fetchCurrentCaptain() {
                const deptId = departmentSelect.value;
                const sportId = sportSelect.value;

                if (deptId && sportId) {
                    try {
                        const response = await fetch(`/api/players/captain?deptId=${deptId}&sportId=${sportId}`);
                        if (response.ok) {
                            const data = await response.json();
                            if (data.captain) {
                                currentCaptainNameSpan.textContent = data.captain.fullName;
                                currentCaptainIdSpan.textContent = data.captain.playerID;
                                newCaptainFullNameInput.value = data.captain.fullName; 
                                captainInfoDiv.style.display = 'block';
                            } else {
                                currentCaptainNameSpan.textContent = 'N/A';
                                currentCaptainIdSpan.textContent = 'N/A';
                                newCaptainFullNameInput.value = ''; 
                                captainInfoDiv.style.display = 'none';
                            }
                        } else {
                            console.error('Error fetching current captain:', response.statusText);
                            captainInfoDiv.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    } catch (error) {
                        console.error('Fetch error:', error);
                        captainInfoDiv.style.display = 'none';
                    }
                } else {
                    captainInfoDiv.style.display = 'none';
                }
            }

            departmentSelect.addEventListener('change', fetchCurrentCaptain);
            sportSelect.addEventListener('change', fetchCurrentCaptain);

            
            if (departmentSelect.value && sportSelect.value) {
                fetchCurrentCaptain();
            }
        });
    </script>
}

                    <option value="">All Categories</option>
                    <option value="0">Boys</option>
                    <option value="1">Girls</option>
                </select>
            </div>
            <button class="btn btn-sm btn-primary" ng-click="loadPoints()" ng-disabled="isLoading">
                <span ng-show="!isLoading"><i class="bi bi-arrow-clockwise"></i> Refresh</span>
                <span ng-show="isLoading" class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm" role="status" aria-hidden="true"></span>
            </button>
        </div>
    </div>

    <div class="table-responsive">
        <table class="table table-striped table-hover table-bordered shadow-sm">
            <thead class="table-cust-header">
                <tr>
                    <th class="text-center" style="width: 10%;">Rank</th>
                    <th ng-click="sortBy('deptName')" style="cursor: pointer;">
                        Department
                        <i class="bi" ng-class="{'bi-caret-down-fill': sortColumn === 'deptName' && !sortReverse, 'bi-caret-up-fill': sortColumn === 'deptName' && sortReverse}"></i>
                    </th>
                    <th class="text-center" ng-click="sortBy('totalPoints')" style="cursor: pointer; width: 20%;">
                        Total Points
                        <i class="bi" ng-class="{'bi-caret-down-fill': sortColumn === 'totalPoints' && !sortReverse, 'bi-caret-up-fill': sortColumn === 'totalPoints' && sortReverse}"></i>
                    </th>
                </tr>
            </thead>
            <tbody>
                <tr ng-if="isLoading">
                    <td colspan="3" class="text-center">
                        <div class="spinner-border text-primary my-3" role="status">
                            <span class="visually-hidden">Loading...</span>
                        </div>
                        <p>Loading Points...</p>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr ng-if="!isLoading && departments.length === 0">
                    <td colspan="3" class="text-center">
                        <div class="alert alert-info" role="alert">
                            No departments found or points not yet calculated.
                        </div>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr ng-repeat-start="dept in departments | orderBy:sortColumn:sortReverse" ng-click="toggleDetails(dept)" style="cursor: pointer;" title="Click to view details" class="dept-row">
                    <td class="text-center align-middle">
                        <span ng-if="$index === 0" class="text-warning me-2" style="font-size: 1.5em;" title="First Place">&#127942;</span>
                        {{ $index + 1 }}
                    </td>
                    <td class="align-middle">
                        <div class="d-flex align-items-center">
                            <i class="bi me-2 text-muted" ng-class="{'bi-chevron-right': !dept.showDetails, 'bi-chevron-down': dept.showDetails}"></i>
                            <img ng-if="dept.logoUrl" ng-src="{{dept.logoUrl}}" alt="{{dept.deptName}} Logo" class="mx-2" style="height: 30px; width: 30px; object-fit: contain;">
                            {{ dept.deptName }}
                        </div>
                    </td>
                    <td class="text-center align-middle">
                        <strong>{{ dept.totalPoints }}</strong>
                    </td>
                </tr>
                <tr ng-repeat-end ng-show="dept.showDetails">
                    <td colspan="3" class="p-0 bg-light">
                        <div class="p-3">
                            <h6 class="text-primary mb-3">Points Breakdown for {{ dept.deptName }}</h6>
                            
                            <div ng-if="dept.loadingDetails" class="text-center py-2">
                                <div class="spinner-border spinner-border-sm text-secondary" role="status"></div> Loading details...
                            </div>

                            <div ng-if="!dept.loadingDetails && dept.matchDetails && dept.matchDetails.length === 0" class="alert alert-warning m-0">
                                No finished matches found contributing to points yet.
                            </div>

                            <div ng-if="!dept.loadingDetails && dept.matchDetails && dept.matchDetails.length > 0" class="table-responsive">
                                <table class="table table-sm table-bordered mb-0 bg-white">
                                    <thead class="table-light">
                                        <tr>
                                            <th>Date</th>
                                            <th>Sport & Category</th>
                                            <th>Opponent</th>
                                            <th>Score</th>
                                            <th>Result</th>
                                            <th class="text-center">Points</th>
                                        </tr>
                                    </thead>
                                    <tbody>
                                        <tr ng-repeat="match in dept.matchDetails">
                                            <td>{{ match.matchDate }}</td>
                                            <td>
                                                <div class="fw-bold">{{ match.sportName }}</div>
                                                <span class="badge" ng-class="{'bg-primary': match.category === 'Boys', 'bg-danger': match.category === 'Girls'}" style="font-size: 0.7rem;">{{ match.category }}</span>
                                            </td>
                                            <td>{{ match.opponent || 'N/A' }}</td>
                                            <td>{{ match.score }}</td>
                                            <td>
                                                <span class="badge rounded-pill" 
                                                      ng-class="{'bg-success': match.result === 'Win', 'bg-secondary': match.result === 'Draw', 'bg-danger': match.result === 'Loss'}">
                                                    {{ match.result }}
                                                </span>
                                            </td>
                                            <td class="text-center fw-bold">{{ match.points }}</td>
                                        </tr>
                                    </tbody>
                                </table>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </td>
                </tr>
            </tbody>
        </table>
    </div>
</div>

                                <td>@(match.DepartmentA?.DeptName ?? "TBD")</td>
                                <td>@(match.DepartmentB?.DeptName ?? "TBD")</td>
                                <td>@(match.ScoreA ?? "N/A") - @(match.ScoreB ?? "N/A")</td>
                                <td>@match.Status</td>
                            </tr>
                        }
                    </tbody>
                </table>
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="alert alert-info" role="alert">
                    No matches scheduled for today.
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        document.addEventListener('DOMContentLoaded', function () {
            const btnAskAI = document.getElementById('btnAskAI');
            const aiQuery = document.getElementById('aiQuery');
            const aiResponseContainer = document.getElementById('aiResponseContainer');
            const aiResponseText = document.getElementById('aiResponseText');
            const aiLoading = document.getElementById('aiLoading');
            const aiCard = document.getElementById('aiSearchCard');

            function expandAI() {
                aiCard.classList.add('active');
            }

            function collapseAI() {
                aiCard.classList.remove('active');
            }

            aiQuery.addEventListener('focus', expandAI);
            

            document.addEventListener('click', function(e) {
                if (!aiCard.contains(e.target)) {
                    collapseAI();
                }
            });
            
            document.addEventListener('keydown', function(e) {
                if (e.key === 'Escape' && aiCard.classList.contains('active')) {
                    collapseAI();
                    aiQuery.blur();
                }
            });

            function formatAIResponse(text) {
                if (!text) return "";

                let safe = text.replace(/&/g, "&amp;").replace(/</g, "&lt;").replace(/>/g, "&gt;");
                

                safe = safe.replace(/\*\*(.*?)\*\*/g, '<strong>$1</strong>');
                




                safe = safe.replace(/^[\*\-]\s+(.*)$/gm, '<li>$1</li>');
                


                safe = safe.replace(/\n/g, '<br>');
                
                return safe;
            }


            const btnClearAI = document.getElementById('btnClearAI');
            if (btnClearAI) {
                btnClearAI.addEventListener('click', function() {
                    aiResponseContainer.classList.add('d-none');
                    aiQuery.value = '';
                });
            }


            const categoryFilter = document.getElementById('categoryFilter');
            if (categoryFilter) {
                categoryFilter.addEventListener('change', function() {
                    const selected = this.value;
                    const rows = document.querySelectorAll('.match-row');
                    rows.forEach(row => {
                        if (selected === 'All' || row.dataset.category === selected) {
                            row.style.display = '';
                        } else {
                            row.style.display = 'none';
                        }
                    });
                });
            }

            btnAskAI.addEventListener('click', async function () {
                const query = aiQuery.value.trim();
                if (!query) return;


                aiResponseContainer.classList.add('d-none');
                aiLoading.classList.remove('d-none');
                btnAskAI.disabled = true;

                try {
                    const response = await fetch('/Home/AskAI', {
                        method: 'POST',
                        headers: {
                            'Content-Type': 'application/json',
                        },
                        body: JSON.stringify(query)
                    });

                    if (response.ok) {
                        const data = await response.json();
                        aiResponseText.innerHTML = formatAIResponse(data.answer);
                        aiResponseContainer.classList.remove('d-none');
                    } else {
                        aiResponseText.innerText = "Sorry, I couldn't process your request right now.";
                        aiResponseContainer.classList.remove('d-none');
                    }
                } catch (error) {
                    console.error('AI Error:', error);
                    aiResponseText.innerText = "An error occurred while connecting to the AI service.";
                    aiResponseContainer.classList.remove('d-none');
                } finally {
                    aiLoading.classList.add('d-none');
                    btnAskAI.disabled = false;
                }
            });
        });

        var app = angular.module('sportsPortalApp', []);

        app.controller('liveTickerController', function ($scope, $http, $interval) {
            $scope.liveTickerContent = "Loading live scores...";
            $scope.liveIndicator = false;

            function fetchLiveScores() {
                $http.get('/Home/GetLiveMatches')
                    .then(function (response) {
                        var liveMatches = response.data;
                        if (liveMatches && liveMatches.length > 0) {

                            var liveMatch = liveMatches.find(m => m.status === "Live");
                            if (liveMatch) {
                                $scope.liveTickerContent = `${liveMatch.departmentA_Name} vs ${liveMatch.departmentB_Name} - ${liveMatch.scoreA ?? 'N/A'} : ${liveMatch.scoreB ?? 'N/A'}`;
                                $scope.liveIndicator = true;
                            } else {

                                var nextMatch = liveMatches.sort((a, b) => new Date(a.matchDateTime) - new Date(b.matchDateTime))[0];
                                if (nextMatch) {
                                    $scope.liveTickerContent = `Next Match: ${nextMatch.departmentA_Name} vs ${nextMatch.departmentB_Name} ${nextMatch.timeRemaining ? '(' + nextMatch.timeRemaining + ')' : ''}`;
                                    $liveIndicator = false;
                                } else {
                                    $scope.liveTickerContent = "No live or upcoming matches at the moment.";
                                    $scope.liveIndicator = false;
                                }
                            }
                        } else {
                            $scope.liveTickerContent = "No live or upcoming matches at the moment.";
                            $scope.liveIndicator = false;
                        }
                    }, function (error) {
                        console.error("Error fetching live scores:", error);
                        $scope.liveTickerContent = "Failed to load live scores.";
                        $scope.liveIndicator = false;
                    });
            }

            fetchLiveScores();
            $interval(fetchLiveScores, 30000); 
        });
    </script>
}

                        </div>

                        <div class="mb-3">

                            <select asp-for="Category" class="form-select">
                                <option value="General">General</option>
                                <option value="Cricket">Cricket</option>
                                <option value="Futsal">Futsal</option>
                                <option value="Badminton">Badminton</option>
                                <option value="Table Tennis">Table Tennis</option>
                                <option value="Volleyball">Volleyball</option>
                                <option value="Prize Distribution">Prize Distribution</option>
                            </select>
                            <span asp-validation-for="Category" class="text-danger"></span>
                        </div>

                        <div class="mb-4">
                            <label class="form-label">Select Image</label>
                            <input type="file" name="ImageFile" class="form-control" accept="image/*" required onchange="previewImage(this)"/>
                            <span class="text-danger field-validation-valid" data-valmsg-for="ImageFile" data-valmsg-replace="true"></span>
                        </div>

                        
                        <div class="mb-4 text-center d-none" id="previewContainer">
                            <img id="imgPreview" src="#" alt="Preview" class="img-fluid rounded shadow-sm" style="max-height: 200px;" />
                        </div>

                        <div class="d-grid gap-2">
                            <button type="submit" class="btn btn-primary btn-lg rounded-pill">Upload</button>
                            <a asp-action="Index" class="btn btn-light rounded-pill">Cancel</a>
                        </div>
                    </form>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Scripts {
    @{await Html.RenderPartialAsync("_ValidationScriptsPartial");}
    <script>
        function previewImage(input) {
            if (input.files && input.files[0]) {
                var reader = new FileReader();
                reader.onload = function(e) {
                    $('#imgPreview').attr('src', e.target.result);
                    $('#previewContainer').removeClass('d-none');
                }
                reader.readAsDataURL(input.files[0]);
            }
        }
    </script>
}


./Views/Gallery/Index.cshtml
@model IEnumerable<SportsPortal.Models.GalleryImage>

@{
    ViewData["Title"] = "Event Gallery";
    var categories = ViewBag.Categories as List<string>;
    var currentCategory = ViewBag.CurrentCategory as string;
}

<div class="container py-4">
    <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center mb-4">
        <h1 class="display-4 text-primary fw-bold">Event Gallery</h1>
        @if (User.IsInRole("Organizer"))
        {
            <a asp-action="Upload" class="btn btn-primary rounded-pill px-4"><i class="bi bi-cloud-upload me-2"></i>Upload Photo</a>
        }
    </div>

    
    <div class="mb-4">
        <div class="d-flex gap-2 flex-wrap">
            <a asp-action="Index" asp-route-category="All" class="btn btn-sm rounded-pill px-3 @(currentCategory == "All" ? "btn-dark" : "btn-outline-dark")">All</a>
            @if (categories != null)
            {
                foreach (var cat in categories)
                {
                    <a asp-action="Index" asp-route-category="@cat" class="btn btn-sm rounded-pill px-3 @(currentCategory == cat ? "btn-dark" : "btn-outline-dark")">@cat</a>
                }
            }
        </div>
    </div>

    @if (Model.Any())
    {
        <div class="gallery-grid">
            @foreach (var item in Model)
            {
                <div class="gallery-item mb-3 break-inside-avoid">
                    <div class="card border-0 shadow-sm overflow-hidden position-relative group-hover">
                        <img src="@item.ImagePath" class="img-fluid w-100" alt="@item.Title" style="cursor: pointer;" onclick="openLightbox(this)">
                        
                        
                        <div class="gallery-overlay position-absolute bottom-0 start-0 w-100 p-3 bg-dark bg-opacity-75 text-white" style="transform: translateY(100%); transition: transform 0.3s ease;">
                            <h6 class="mb-0">@item.Title</h6>
                            <small class="text-white-50">@item.Category</small>
                            @if (User.IsInRole("Organizer"))
                            {
                                <form asp-action="Delete" asp-route-id="@item.ImageID" method="post" class="mt-2 d-inline-block" onsubmit="return confirm('Delete this image?');">
                                    <button type="submit" class="btn btn-danger btn-sm py-0 px-2" style="font-size: 0.7rem;">Delete</button>
                                </form>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    }
    else
    {
        <div class="text-center py-5 text-muted">
            <i class="bi bi-images display-1 d-block mb-3 opacity-25"></i>
            <h3>No photos yet</h3>
            <p>Check back later for event highlights!</p>
        </div>
    }
</div>


<div class="modal fade" id="lightboxModal" tabindex="-1" aria-hidden="true">
    <div class="modal-dialog modal-dialog-centered modal-xl">
        <div class="modal-content bg-transparent border-0">
            <div class="modal-body p-0 text-center position-relative">
                <button type="button" class="btn-close btn-close-white position-absolute top-0 end-0 m-3 z-3" data-bs-dismiss="modal" aria-label="Close"></button>
                <img id="lightboxImage" src="" class="img-fluid rounded shadow-lg" style="max-height: 90vh;">
            </div>
        </div>
    </div>
</div>

@section Styles {
    <style>
        .gallery-grid {
            column-count: 1;
            column-gap: 1rem;
        }
        @@media (min-width: 576px) { .gallery-grid { column-count: 2; } }
        @@media (min-width: 992px) { .gallery-grid { column-count: 3; } }
        
        .break-inside-avoid { break-inside: avoid; }
        
        .gallery-item:hover .gallery-overlay {
            transform: translateY(0) !important;
        }
    </style>
}

@section Scripts {
    <script>
        function openLightbox(img) {
            var src = img.getAttribute("src");
            document.getElementById("lightboxImage").setAttribute("src", src);
            var myModal = new bootstrap.Modal(document.getElementById('lightboxModal'));
            myModal.show();
        }
    </script>
}

                <div class="col-md-6">
                    <div class="card shadow-sm h-100 border-0 rounded-4 overflow-hidden">
                        <div class="card-header bg-white border-bottom py-3">
                            <h4 class="mb-0 text-secondary fw-bold"><i class="bi bi-calendar-event me-2 text-primary"></i>Upcoming</h4>
                        </div>
                        <div class="card-body p-0">
                            @if (Model.UpcomingMatches.Any())
                            {
                                <div class="list-group list-group-flush">
                                    @foreach (var match in Model.UpcomingMatches)
                                    {
                                        <div class="list-group-item py-3 px-3">

                                                <div class="small">
                                                    <span class="fw-bold">@match.DepartmentA?.DeptName</span> 
                                                    <span class="text-muted px-1">vs</span> 
                                                    <span class="fw-bold">@match.DepartmentB?.DeptName</span>
                                                </div>
                                                <span class="badge bg-light text-primary border rounded-pill small">@match.MatchDate.ToString("MMM dd")</span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    }
                                </div>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <div class="p-4 text-center text-muted small">
                                    No upcoming matches.
                                </div>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>

                
                <div class="col-md-6">
                    <div class="card shadow-sm h-100 border-0 rounded-4 overflow-hidden">
                        <div class="card-header bg-white border-bottom py-3">
                            <h4 class="mb-0 text-secondary fw-bold"><i class="bi bi-check-circle me-2 text-success"></i>Results</h4>
                        </div>
                        <div class="card-body p-0">
                            @if (Model.CompletedMatches.Any())
                            {
                                <div class="list-group list-group-flush">
                                    @foreach (var match in Model.CompletedMatches)
                                    {
                                        <div class="list-group-item py-3 px-3">
                                            <div class="d-flex justify-content-between align-items-center">
                                                <div class="small text-truncate" style="max-width: 70%;">
                                                    <span>@match.DepartmentA?.DeptName</span> 
                                                    <span class="text-muted px-1">vs</span> 
                                                    <span>@match.DepartmentB?.DeptName</span>
                                                </div>
                                                <span class="fw-bold text-success">@match.ScoreA-@match.ScoreB</span>
                                            </div>
                                        </div>
                                    }
                                </div>
                            }
                            else
                            {
                                <div class="p-4 text-center text-muted small">
                                    No results yet.
                                </div>
                            }
                        </div>
                    </div>
                </div>
            </div>
        </div>

        
        <div class="tab-pane fade" id="players" role="tabpanel" aria-labelledby="players-tab">
            <h4 class="mb-4 text-secondary fw-bold px-2"><i class="bi bi-people me-2 text-primary"></i>Participating Teams</h4>
            @if (Model.Players.Any())
            {
                var teams = Model.Players.GroupBy(p => p.Department).OrderBy(g => g.Key.DeptName);
                foreach (var team in teams)
                {
                    <div class="card shadow-sm mb-4 border-0 rounded-4 overflow-hidden">
                        <div class="card-header bg-light border-0 py-3">
                            <div class="d-flex align-items-center justify-content-between">
                                <h5 class="mb-0 fw-bold text-primary">@team.Key.DeptName</h5>
                                <span class="badge bg-white text-primary border rounded-pill px-3">@team.Count() Players</span>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                        <div class="card-body p-0">
                            <div class="table-responsive">
                                <table class="table table-hover align-middle mb-0">
                                    <thead class="table-light">
                                        <tr>
                                            <th style="width: 40%;" class="ps-4">Name</th>
                                            <th style="width: 30%;">Reg Number</th>
                                            <th style="width: 30%;">Role</th>
                                        </tr>
                                    </thead>
                                    <tbody>
                                        @foreach (var player in team)
                                        {
                                            <tr>
                                                <td class="fw-bold ps-4">@player.FullName</td>
                                                <td>@player.RegNumber</td>
                                                <td>
                                                    @if (player.IsCaptain)
                                                    {
                                                        <span class="badge bg-warning text-dark rounded-pill px-3"><i class="bi bi-star-fill me-1"></i>Captain</span>
                                                    }
                                                    else
                                                    {
                                                        <span class="text-muted small">Player</span>
                                                    }
                                                </td>
                                            </tr>
                                        }
                                    </tbody>
                                </table>
                            </div>
                        </div>
                    </div>
                }
            }
            else
            {
                <div class="alert alert-info text-center rounded-4 py-5 border-0">
                    <i class="bi bi-info-circle display-4 d-block mb-3 opacity-50"></i>
                    No players registered for this sport yet.
                </div>
            }
        </div>
    </div>
</div>
